      "description": "<p>In the Land of the Mists, power and dread lie in the simple question &ldquo;What happened to me?&rdquo;</p>\r\n<p class=\"characters-statblock\" style=\"font-family: Roboto Condensed;\"><strong>Lineages</strong><br />+2 to an Ability Score and +1 to One Other Ability Score, or, +1 to Three Different Ability Scores</p><p>Where wishing fails, ancient magic can offer a heart&rsquo;s desire&mdash;at least, for a time. Hexbloods are individuals infused with eldritch magic, fey energy, or mysterious witchcraft. Some who enter into bargains with hags gain their deepest wishes but eventually find themselves transformed. These changes evidence a hag&rsquo;s influence: ears that split in forked points, skin in lurid shades, long hair that regrows if cut, and an irremovable living crown. Along with these marks, hexbloods manifest hag-like traits, such as [sense]darkvision[/sense] and a variety of magical methods to beguile the senses and avoid the same.</p>\r\n<p>While many hexbloods gain their lineage after making a deal with a hag, others reveal their nature as they age&mdash;particularly if a hag influenced them early in life or even before their birth. Many hexbloods turn to lives of adventure, seeking to discover the mysteries of their magic, to forge a connection with their fey natures, or to avoid a hag that obsesses over them.</p>\r\n<h4 id=\"HeirofHags\" class=\"compendium-hr\">Heir of Hags</h4>\r\n<p>One way hags create more of their kind is through the creation of hexbloods. Every hexblood exhibits features suggestive of the hag whose magic inspires their powers. This includes an unusual crown, often called an eldercross or a witch&rsquo;s turn. This living, garland-like part of a hexblood&rsquo;s body extends from their temples and wraps behind the head, serving as a visible mark of the bargain between hag and hexblood, a debt owed, or a change to come.</p>\r\n<h4 id=\"HexbloodOrigins\" class=\"compendium-hr\">Hexblood Origins</h4>\r\n<p>A bargain with a hag or other eerie forces transformed your character into a magical being. Roll on or choose an option from the Hexblood Origins table to determine how your character gained their lineage.</p>\r\n<h5 id=\"HexbloodOrigins\" class=\"compendium-hr quick-menu-exclude\">Hexblood Origins</h5>\r\n<div class=\"table-overflow-wrapper\">\r\n<table class=\"compendium-left-aligned-table\">\r\n<thead>\r\n<tr>\r\n<th>d6</th>\r\n<th>Origin</th>\r\n</tr>\r\n</thead>\r\n<tbody>\r\n<tr>\r\n<td>1</td>\r\n<td>Seeking a child, your parent made a bargain with a hag. You are the result of that arrangement.</td>\r\n</tr>\r\n<tr>\r\n<td>2</td>\r\n<td>Fey kidnappers swapped you and your parents&rsquo; child.</td>\r\n</tr>\r\n<tr>\r\n<td>3</td>\r\n<td>A coven of hags lost one of its members. You were created to replace the lost hag.</td>\r\n</tr>\r\n<tr>\r\n<td>4</td>\r\n<td>You were cursed as a child. A deal with the spirits of the forest transformed you into a hexblood, now free of the curse.</td>\r\n</tr>\r\n<tr>\r\n<td>5</td>\r\n<td>You began life as a fey creature, but an accident changed you and forced you from your home.</td>\r\n</tr>\r\n<tr>\r\n<td>6</td>\r\n<td>A slighted druid transformed you and bound you to live only so long as a sacred tree bears fruit.</td>\r\n</tr>\r\n</tbody>\r\n</table>\r\n</div>\r\n<h4 id=\"HexbloodsintheDomainsofDread\" class=\"compendium-hr\">Hexbloods in the Domains of Dread</h4>\r\n<p>When creating a hexblood, consult with your DM to see if it&rsquo;s appropriate to tie your origins to one of the following Domains of Dread (detailed in chapter 3):</p>\r\n<p><strong><a title=\"Hazlan\" href=\"https://www.dndbeyond.com/sources/vrgtr/hazlan/\">Hazlan</a>.</strong> The bizarre magic of this crumbling domain exposes the populace to supernatural forces, occasionally giving rise to hexbloods.</p>\r\n<p><strong><a title=\"Kartakass\" href=\"https://www.dndbeyond.com/sources/vrgtr/kartakass/\">Kartakass</a>.</strong> Whimsical witches make their homes in the forests of Kartakass. They eagerly grant the wishes of locals seeking grand fortunes for their children.</p>\r\n<p><strong><a title=\"Tepest\" href=\"https://www.dndbeyond.com/sources/vrgtr/tepest/\">Tepest</a>.</strong> Many of the children in the town of Viktal are hexbloods who exhibit their supernatural natures from a young age. Each youngster is considered a gift from the town&rsquo;s patron deity, who is known as Mother.</p>\r\n<blockquote>\r\n<p><strong>BECOMING A HAG</strong></p>\r\n<p>Hags can undertake a ritual to irreversibly transform a hexblood they created into a new hag, either one of their own kind or that embodies the hexblood&rsquo;s nature. This requires that both the hag and hexblood be in the same place and consent to the lengthy ritual&mdash;circumstances most hexbloods shun but might come to accept over the course of centuries. Once a hexblood undergoes this irreversible ritual, they emerge as a hag NPC no longer under the control of the hexblood&rsquo;s player, unless the DM rules otherwise.</p>\r\n</blockquote>",
